---
title     : "Typed: Raw terms with types (broken)"
layout    : page
permalink : /Typed
---

This version uses raw terms. Substitution presumes that no
generation of fresh names is required.

The substitution algorithm is based on one by McBride.
It is given a map from names to terms. Say the mapping of a
name is trivial if it takes a name to a term consisting of
just the variable with that name. No fresh names are required
if the mapping on each variable is either trivial or to a
closed term. However, the proof of correctness currently
contains a hole, and may be difficult to repair.

## Values do not reduce

Values do not reduce.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="Val-⟶"></a><a id="11744" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11744" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="11750" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11752" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="11754" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11755" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11755" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="11757" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11757" class="Bound">N</a><a id="11758" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11760" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11762" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#7911" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="11768" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11755" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="11770" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11772" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="11774" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11775" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11755" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="11777" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#8178" class="Datatype Operator">⟶</a> <a id="11779" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11757" class="Bound">N</a><a id="11780" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="11782" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11744" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="11788" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#8061" class="InductiveConstructor">Fun</a> <a id="11792" class="Symbol">()</a>
<a id="11795" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11744" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="11801" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#7939" class="InductiveConstructor">Zero</a> <a id="11806" class="Symbol">()</a>
<a id="11809" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11744" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="11815" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11816" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#7984" class="InductiveConstructor">Suc</a> <a id="11820" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11820" class="Bound">VM</a><a id="11822" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11824" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11825" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#8493" class="InductiveConstructor">ξ-suc</a> <a id="11831" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11831" class="Bound">M⟶N</a><a id="11834" class="Symbol">)</a>  <a id="11837" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="11840" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11744" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="11846" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11820" class="Bound">VM</a> <a id="11849" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11831" class="Bound">M⟶N</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

As a corollary, terms that reduce are not values.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="⟶-Val"></a><a id="11928" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11928" class="Function">⟶-Val</a> <a id="11934" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11936" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="11938" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11939" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11939" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="11941" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11941" class="Bound">N</a><a id="11942" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11944" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11946" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11947" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11939" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="11949" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#8178" class="Datatype Operator">⟶</a> <a id="11951" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11941" class="Bound">N</a><a id="11952" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11954" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11956" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="11958" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#7911" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="11964" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11939" class="Bound">M</a>
<a id="11966" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11928" class="Function">⟶-Val</a> <a id="11972" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11972" class="Bound">M⟶N</a> <a id="11976" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11976" class="Bound">VM</a>  <a id="11980" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="11983" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11744" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="11989" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11976" class="Bound">VM</a> <a id="11992" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11972" class="Bound">M⟶N</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Reduction is deterministic

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="det"></a><a id="12052" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#12052" class="Function">det</a> <a id="12056" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12058" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="12060" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12061" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#12061" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="12063" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#12063" class="Bound">M′</a> <a id="12066" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#12066" class="Bound">M″</a><a id="12068" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="12072" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12074" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12075" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#12061" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="12077" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#8178" class="Datatype Operator">⟶</a> <a id="12079" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#12063" class="Bound">M′</a><a id="12081" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="12085" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12087" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12088" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#12061" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="12090" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#8178" class="Datatype Operator">⟶</a> <a id="12092" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#12066" class="Bound">M″</a><a id="12094" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="12100" class="Comment">----------</a>

<a id="13522" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#12052" class="Function">det</a> <a id="13526" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13527" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#9254" class="InductiveConstructor">β-Y</a> <a id="13531" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a><a id="13535" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13537" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13538" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#9182" class="InductiveConstructor">ξ-Y</a> <a id="13542" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#13542" class="Bound">M⟶M″</a><a id="13546" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13548" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13550" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Empty.html#360" class="Function">⊥-elim</a> <a id="13557" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13558" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#11744" class="Function">Val-⟶</a> <a id="13564" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#8061" class="InductiveConstructor">Fun</a> <a id="13568" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#13542" class="Bound">M⟶M″</a><a id="13572" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="13574" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#12052" class="Function">det</a> <a id="13578" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13579" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#9254" class="InductiveConstructor">β-Y</a> <a id="13583" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a><a id="13587" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13589" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13590" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#9254" class="InductiveConstructor">β-Y</a> <a id="13594" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a><a id="13598" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13600" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13602" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#140" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Almost half the lines in the above proof are redundant, for example

    det (ξ-·₁ L⟶L′) (ξ-·₂ VL _) = ⊥-elim (Val-⟶ VL L⟶L′)
    det (ξ-·₂ VL _) (ξ-·₁ L⟶L″) = ⊥-elim (Val-⟶ VL L⟶L″)
 
are essentially identical. What we might like to do is delete the
redundant lines and add

    det M⟶M′ M⟶M″ = sym (det M⟶M″ M⟶M′)

to the bottom of the proof. But this does not work. The termination
checker complains, because the arguments have merely switched order
and neither is smaller.

## Canonical forms

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="14130" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Canonical"></a><a id="14135" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#14135" class="Datatype">Canonical</a> <a id="14145" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14147" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#1720" class="Datatype">Term</a> <a id="14152" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14154" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#1585" class="Datatype">Type</a> <a id="14159" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14161" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="14165" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="Canonical.Zero"></a><a id="14174" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#14174" class="InductiveConstructor">Zero</a> <a id="14179" class="Symbol">:</a> 
      <a id="14188" class="Comment">-------------------</a>
      <a id="14214" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#14135" class="Datatype">Canonical</a> <a id="14224" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#1845" class="InductiveConstructor">`zero</a> <a id="14230" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#1604" class="InductiveConstructor">`ℕ</a>

  <a id="Canonical.Suc"></a><a id="14236" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#14236" class="InductiveConstructor">Suc</a> <a id="14240" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14242" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="14244" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14245" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#14245" class="Bound">V</a><a id="14246" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="14252" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14254" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#14135" class="Datatype">Canonical</a> <a id="14264" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#14245" class="Bound">V</a> <a id="14266" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#1604" class="InductiveConstructor">`ℕ</a>
      <a id="14275" class="Comment">----------------------</a>

## Preservation

### Domain of an environment

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="16686" class="Comment">{-
dom : Env → List Id
dom ε            =  []
dom (Γ , x `: A)  =  x ∷ dom Γ

dom-lemma : ∀ {Γ y B} → Γ ∋ y `: B → y ∈ dom Γ
dom-lemma Z           =  here
dom-lemma (S x≢y ⊢y)  =  there (dom-lemma ⊢y)

free-lemma : ∀ {Γ M A} → Γ ⊢ M `: A → free M ⊆ dom Γ
free-lemma (Ax ⊢x) w∈ with w∈
...                      | here         =  dom-lemma ⊢x
...                      | there ()   
free-lemma {Γ} (⊢λ {N = N} ⊢N)          =  ∷-to-\\ (free-lemma ⊢N)
free-lemma (⊢L · ⊢M) w∈ with ++-to-⊎ w∈
...                        | inj₁ ∈L    = free-lemma ⊢L ∈L
...                        | inj₂ ∈M    = free-lemma ⊢M ∈M
free-lemma ⊢zero ()
free-lemma (⊢suc ⊢M) w∈                 = free-lemma ⊢M w∈
free-lemma (⊢pred ⊢M) w∈                = free-lemma ⊢M w∈
free-lemma (⊢if0 ⊢L ⊢M ⊢N) w∈
        with ++-to-⊎ w∈
...         | inj₁ ∈L                   = free-lemma ⊢L ∈L
...         | inj₂ ∈MN with ++-to-⊎ ∈MN
...                       | inj₁ ∈M     = free-lemma ⊢M ∈M
...                       | inj₂ ∈N     = free-lemma ⊢N ∈N
free-lemma (⊢Y ⊢M) w∈                   = free-lemma ⊢M w∈       
-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

<a id="19740" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#18667" class="Function">⊢subst</a> <a id="19747" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#19747" class="Bound">⊢ρ</a> <a id="19750" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19751" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#2952" class="InductiveConstructor">⊢Y</a> <a id="19754" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#19754" class="Bound">⊢M</a><a id="19756" class="Symbol">)</a>                <a id="19773" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="19776" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#2952" class="InductiveConstructor">⊢Y</a> <a id="19779" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19780" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#18667" class="Function">⊢subst</a> <a id="19787" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#19747" class="Bound">⊢ρ</a> <a id="19790" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Typed.md %}{% raw %}#19754" class="Bound">⊢M</a><a id="19792" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Let's look at examples.  Assume `M` is closed.  Example 1.

    subst (∅ , "x" ↦ M) (`λ "y" `→ ` "x")  ≡  `λ "y" `→ M

Example 2.

      subst (∅ , "y" ↦ ` "y" , "x" ↦ M) (`λ "y" `→ ` "x" · ` "y")
    ≡
      `λ "y" `→ subst (∅ , "y" ↦ ` "y" , "x" ↦ M , "y" ↦ ` "y") (` "x" · ` "y")
    ≡
      `λ "y" `→ (M · ` "y")

The hypotheses of the theorem appear to be violated. Drat!
